**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Flow-control statements: if, while, for</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895777792;margin-left:0px;margin-top:22px;width:93px;height:18px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image048.jpg" width="93" height="18" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:9.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">if-elif-else</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895776768;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image032.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">if </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">name == </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Monica'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Hi, Monica.'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">elif </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">age &lt; </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">12</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'You are not Monica, kiddo.'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">else</span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'You are neither Monica nor a little kid.'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895775744;margin-left:0px;margin-top:37px;width:30px;height:18px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image049.jpg" width="30" height="18" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:9.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895774720;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:357px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image050.jpg" width="967" height="357" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Looping over a string </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">c **in** </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"abcdefg"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(c)</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Looping over a range </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'My name is'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">) **for** i **in** range(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">5</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">):</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Carlita Cinco ('</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> + str(i) + </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">')'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Looping over a list</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">lst = \[</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">0</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">i **in** lst:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(i)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Looping over a dictionary</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">spam = {</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'color'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">: </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'red'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'age'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">: </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">42</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">v **in** spam.values():</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(v)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Loop over a list of tuples and</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Destructuring to values</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Assuming spam.items returns a list of tuples</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Each containing two values (k, v)</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">k, v **in** spam.items():</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Key: '</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> + k + </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">' Value: '</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> + str(v))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:9.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">while </span><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> break </span><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">and</span><span style="font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> continue</span>**

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895773696"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-15px;
width:194px;height:18px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image051.jpg" width="194" height="18" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">while </span><span style="font-size:
8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">loop as long as the condition is</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333"> True </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895772672"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-13px;
width:36px;height:15px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image052.jpg" width="36" height="15" /></span></span><span style="position:
relative;z-index:-1895771648"><span style="position:absolute;left:192px;
top:-13px;width:30px;height:15px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image008.jpg" width="30" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">break </span><span style="font-size:
8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">allows you to break out of the loop.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895770624"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-13px;
width:36px;height:15px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image015.jpg" width="36" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">continue </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">skips this iteration of the loop and goes to the next iteration.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895769600;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:123px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image053.jpg" width="967" height="123" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895768576"><span style="position:absolute;
left:0px;top:-13px;width:52px;height:15px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image017.jpg" width="52" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">spam = </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">0</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">while </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Hello, world.'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">spam = spam + </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">if </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">spam &lt; </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">5</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">continue</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">break</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Functions</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You use the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> keyword to define a function in Python.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895767552;margin-left:-1px;margin-top:17px;width:969px;height:86px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image054.jpg" width="969" height="86" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895766528"><span style="position:absolute;
left:61px;top:-12px;width:24px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image006.jpg" width="24" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Basic function with no arguments and no return value </span>***<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">printCopyright</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">():</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Copyright 2020. Me, myself and I. All rights reserved."</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Function with positional parameters and a return value</span>*

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page6"></span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">average</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(num1, num2):</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895765504"><span style="position:absolute;left:-1px;top:-10px;
width:969px;height:408px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image055.jpg" width="969" height="408" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(num1/num2)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Calling it with positional arguments</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(average(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">6</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt">               </span>*<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => 3.0</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Calling it with keyword arguments</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">(note that order doesn't matter) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(average(num2=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, num1=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">6</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">));</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Default parameters</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Here the string "Hello" is the default for \`saying\` </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#990000">greeting</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(name, saying=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Hello"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">):</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(saying, name)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">greeting(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Monica"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => Hello Monica</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">greeting(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Monica"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, saying=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Hi"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => Hi Monica</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">A common 'gotcha' is using an mutable object for a default parameter.</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Python doesn't do what you expect. All invocations of the function</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">reference the same mutable object</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Everytime we call this we use the exact same \`itemList\` list</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">appendItem</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(itemName, itemList = \[\]):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">itemList.append(itemName)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">itemList</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(appendItem(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'notebook'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># =></span>*<span style="font-size:10.0pt">   </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">\['notebook'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(appendItem(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'pencil'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># =></span>*<span style="font-size:10.0pt">   </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">\['notebook', 'pencil'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(appendItem(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'eraser'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => \['notebook', 'pencil', 'eraser'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Lambdas</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">In python we have anonymous functions called lambdas, but they are only</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">a single python statement.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895764480;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image018.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">toUpper = **lambda** s: s.upper()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">toUpper(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'hello'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => HELLO</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">is the same as this in JavaScript</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895763456;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image021.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">const </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">toUpper = s => s.toUpperCase();</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">toUpper(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'hello'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">); </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">// # => HELLO</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Errors</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Unlike JavaScript, if you pass the wrong number of arguments to a function</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">it will throw an error.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895762432;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image010.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">average(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => TypeError: average() missing 1 required positional argument: 'num2'</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">average(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => TypeError: average() takes 2 positional arguments but 3 were given</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:14.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Python Learning Objectives (Day 2)</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895761408;margin-left:0px;margin-top:9px;width:967px;height:1px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image001.jpg" width="967" height="1" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Functions</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\* </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">- Get the rest of the position arguments as a tuple</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895760384"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:
relative;z-index:-1895759360"><span style="position:absolute;left:22px;
top:-12px;width:13px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image024.jpg" width="13" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\*\* </span><span style="font-size:8.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">- Get the rest of the keyword arguments as a dictionary</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895758336"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:

top:-12px;width:19px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image056.jpg" width="19" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">variable length positional arguments</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895756288;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:188px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image057.jpg" width="967" height="188" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">add</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(a, b, \*args):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">  </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">args is a tuple of the rest of the arguments </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">total = a + b;</span>

**<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">n **in** args: total += n</span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">total</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">args is None</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">add(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span><span style="font-size:
10.0pt">   </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988"># Returns 3</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># args is (4, 5)</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">add(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">5</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Returns 14</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">variable length keyword arguments</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895755264;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:279px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image058.jpg" width="967" height="279" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">print\_names\_and\_countries</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(greeting, \*\*kwargs):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">  </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">kwargs is a dictionary of the rest of the keyword arguments </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">k, v **in** kwargs.items():</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(greeting, k, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"from"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, v)</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">kwargs would be:</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">{</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'Monica': 'Sweden',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'Charles'='British Virgin Islands',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'Carlo':'Portugal</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">}</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print\_names\_and\_countries(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Hi"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Monica=</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Sweden"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Charles=</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"British Virgin Islands"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Carlo=</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Portugal"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Prints</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Hi Monica from Sweden</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Hi Charles from British Virgin Islands</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Hi Carlo from Portugal</span>*

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page7"></span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">You can combine all of these together</span>

<span style="position:absolute;

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">example2</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(arg\_1, arg\_2, \*args, kw\_1=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">"shark"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, kw\_2=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"blowfish"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, \*\*kwargs):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">pass</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Lists</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Lists are mutable arrays.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895753216;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:162px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image020.jpg" width="967" height="162" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Can be made with square brackets </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">empty\_list = \[\]</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">departments = \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'HR'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Development'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Sales'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Finance'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'IT'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Customer Support'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">\]</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">list built-in function makes a list too</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">specials = list()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">You can use \`in\` to test if something is in the list </span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **in** \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#> True</span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **in** \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#> False</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Dictionaries</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Dictionaries are similar to JavaScript POJOs or </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Map</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> . They have key value pairs.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895752192"><span style="position:absolute;left:0px;top:-12px;
width:967px;height:180px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image059.jpg" width="967" height="180" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># With curlies</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">a = {</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'one'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'two'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'three'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">With the dict built-in function </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">b = dict(one=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, two=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, three=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">You can use the \`in\` operator with dictionaries too</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Sets</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Just like JavaScript's </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">Set</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> , it is an unordered collection of distinct objects.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895751168;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:149px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image026.jpg" width="967" height="149" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895750144"><span style="position:absolute;
left:105px;top:-13px;width:24px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image047.jpg" width="24" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Using curlies (dont' confuse this with dictionaries)</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">school\_bag = {</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'book'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'paper'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'pencil'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'pencil'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'book'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'book'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'book'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'eraser'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Using the set() built in</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">school\_bag = set(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'book'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'paper'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'pencil'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'pencil'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'book'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'book'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'book'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'eraser'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">You can use the \`in\` operator with sets </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **in** {</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#> True</span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333"> print(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **in** {</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988">#> False</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Tuples</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Tuples are *immutable* lists of items.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895749120;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:227px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image060.jpg" width="967" height="227" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># With parenthesis</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">time\_blocks = (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'AM'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'PM'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Without parenthesis</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">colors = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'red'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'blue'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'green'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">numbers = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">with the tuple buit-in function which can also be used to</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">convert things to tuples</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">tuple(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'abc'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span><span style="font-size:10.0pt">               </span>*<span style="font-size:6.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># returns ('a', 'b', 'c')</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">tuple(\[</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\])</span><span style="font-size:
10.0pt">           </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988"># returns (1, 2, 3)</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">you can use the \`in\` operator with tuples </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **in** (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:
122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#> True</span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **in** (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#> False</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Ranges</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">A *range* is simply a list of numbers in order which can't be changed</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">(immutable). Ranges are often used with </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> loops.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895748096"><span style="position:absolute;left:201px;top:-13px;
width:24px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image047.jpg" width="24" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">A </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">range</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> is declared using one to three parameters</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895747072"><span style="position:absolute;left:10px;top:-13px;
width:36px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image035.jpg" width="36" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">start - optional ( </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">0</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> if not supplied) - first number in the sequence</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895746048"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:
relative;z-index:-1895745024"><span style="position:absolute;left:98px;
top:-12px;width:13px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image045.jpg" width="13" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">stop - required - next number past the last number in the sequence</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895744000"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-7px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">step - optional ( </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">1</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> if not supplied) - the difference between each number in</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895742976"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image002.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:
relative;z-index:-1895741952"><span style="position:absolute;left:98px;
top:-12px;width:13px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image045.jpg" width="13" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">the sequence</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">For example</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895740928;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:84px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image019.jpg" width="967" height="84" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>
