<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Built-in functions: filter, map, sorted, enumerate, zip, len, max, min, sum, any, all, dir</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">filter</span>**

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895739904;left:0px;margin-left:45px;margin-top:37px;width:967px;
height:110px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image032.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span><span id="page8"></span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#990000">isOdd</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">(num):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">num % </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">filtered = filter(isOdd, \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\])</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">It returns a filter iterable object</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">but we can cast it to a list </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(list(filtered)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => \[1, 3\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">map</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895738880;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image032.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">toUpper</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(str):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">str.upper()</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">upperCased = map(toUpper, \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'a'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'b'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'c'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\])</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(list(upperCased)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => \['A','B','C'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">sorted</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895737856;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:201px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image061.jpg" width="967" height="201" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sortedItems = sorted(\[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Banana'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'orange'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'apple'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\])</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(list(sortedItems)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => \['Banana', 'apple', 'orange'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Notice Banana is first because uppercase letters come first</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Using a key function to control the sorting and make it sort</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">so the case doesn't matter</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sortedItems = sorted(\[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Banana'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'orange'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'apple'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\], key=str.lower)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(list(sortedItems)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => \['apple', 'Banana', 'orange'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Reversing the sort</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sortedItems = sorted(\[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Banana'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'orange'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'apple'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\], key=str.lower, reverse=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:teal">True</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(list(sortedItems)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => \['orange', 'Banana', 'apple'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">enumerate</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895736832;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:71px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image018.jpg" width="967" height="71" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">quarters = \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'First'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Second'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Third'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Fourth'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(enumerate(quarters))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(enumerate(quarters, start=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">))</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895735808;margin-left:0px;margin-top:34px;width:967px;height:58px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image021.jpg" width="967" height="58" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">0</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'First'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">), (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Second'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">), (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Third'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">), (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Fourth'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'First'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">), (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Second'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">), (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Third'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">), (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Fourth'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">zip</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895734784;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:253px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image062.jpg" width="967" height="253" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">keys = (</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Name"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Email"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">values = (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Bob"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"Bob@bob.com"</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">zipped = zip(keys, values)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(list(zipped))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">=> \[('Name', 'Bob'), ('Email', 'Bob@bob.com')\]</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">You can zip more than two</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">x\_coords = \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">0</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">y\_coords = \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">5</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">5</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">z\_coords = \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">3</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">5</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">4</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">coords = zip(x\_coords, y\_coords, z\_coords)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(list(coords))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => \[(0, 2, 3), (1, 3, 5), (2, 5, 2), (3, 3, 1), (4, 5, 4)\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">dir</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Returns all the attributes of an object including it's methods and dunder methods</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895726592;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:227px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image060.jpg" width="967" height="227" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">user = {</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Name'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'Bob'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'Email'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'bob@bob.com'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">dir(user)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">=> \['\_\_class\_\_', '\_\_contains\_\_', '\_\_delattr\_\_', '\_\_delitem\_\_', '\_\_dir\_\_',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">   </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'\_\_doc\_\_', '\_\_eq\_\_', '\_\_format\_\_', '\_\_ge\_\_', '\_\_getattribute\_\_',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'\_\_getitem\_\_', '\_\_gt\_\_', '\_\_hash\_\_', '\_\_init\_\_', '\_\_init\_subclass\_\_',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'\_\_iter\_\_', '\_\_le\_\_', '\_\_len\_\_', '\_\_lt\_\_', '\_\_ne\_\_', '\_\_new\_\_',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'\_\_reduce\_\_', '\_\_reduce\_ex\_\_', '\_\_repr\_\_', '\_\_reversed\_\_', '\_\_setattr\_\_',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'\_\_setitem\_\_', '\_\_sizeof\_\_', '\_\_str\_\_', '\_\_subclasshook\_\_', 'clear', 'copy',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'fromkeys', 'get', 'items', 'keys', 'pop', 'popitem', 'setdefault',</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">'update', 'values'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Importing packages and modules</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Module - Python code in a file **or** directory</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895725568"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-5px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">Package - A module which is a directory containing a </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">\_\_init\_\_.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> file.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895724544"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-7px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span><span style="position:
relative;z-index:-1895723520"><span style="position:absolute;left:283px;
top:-13px;width:69px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image065.jpg" width="69" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">submodule - A module which is contained within a package</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895722496"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-6px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333">name - an exported function, class or variable in a module</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895721472"><span style="position:absolute;left:9px;top:-7px;
width:3px;height:3px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image064.jpg" width="3" height="3" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Unlike JavaScript, modules export ALL names contained within them without any</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">special </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">export</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> keywords</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895720448"><span style="position:absolute;left:37px;top:-13px;
width:41px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image066.jpg" width="41" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Assuming we have the following package with four submodules</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895719424;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image032.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">math</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">|<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">\_\_init.py</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">|<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">addition.py</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">|<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">subtraction.py</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">|<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">multiplication.py</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">|<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">    </span></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">division.py</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">if we peek into the addition.py file we see there's an add function</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895718400;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image010.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">addition.py</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">We can import \`add\` from other places because it's a \`name\` and is</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">AUTOMATICALLY exported</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">add</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(num1, num2):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">num1 + num2</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Our </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">\_\_init\_\_.py</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333"> has the following lines:</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895717376;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:123px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image053.jpg" width="967" height="123" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895716352"><span style="position:absolute;
left:21px;top:-13px;width:70px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image067.jpg" width="70" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This imports the \`add\` function</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">and now it's also re-exported in here as well! </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.addition **import** add</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">These import and re-export the rest of the functions from the sub modules </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">.subtraction **import** subtract</span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.division **import** divide</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">.multiplication **import** multiply</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Remember any names that exist within a module are automatically exported.</span>*

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895715328;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:4px;height:17px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image068.jpg" width="4" height="17" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#777777">Notice the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#777777">.</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#777777"> syntax because this package can import it's own submodules.</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895714304"><span style="position:absolute;left:72px;top:-13px;
width:13px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image069.jpg" width="13" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">So if we have a </span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;font-family:
&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">script.py</span><span style="font-size:7.5pt;
font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> , and we want to import the add function, we could do it lots of different ways</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895713280;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image010.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895712256"><span style="position:absolute;
left:78px;top:-11px;width:58px;height:14px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image070.jpg" width="58" height="14" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This will load and execute the \`math/\_\_init\_\_.py\` file</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">and give us an object with the exported names in \`math/\_\_init.py\_\_\` </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">import </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">math</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(math.add(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => 3</span>*

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895711232;margin-left:0px;margin-top:35px;width:967px;height:84px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image019.jpg" width="967" height="84" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This imports JUST the add from \`math/\_\_init\_\_.py\` </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">math **import** add</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(add(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => 3</span>*

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895710208;margin-left:0px;margin-top:35px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image010.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This skips importing from \`math/\_\_init\_\_.py\` (although it still runs)</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">and imports directly from the addition.py file</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">math.addition **import** add</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(add(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => 3</span>*

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page10"></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span><span style="position:absolute;z-index:-1895709184;left:0px;margin-left:45px;
margin-top:37px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image010.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">this imports all the functions individually from \`math/\_\_init.py\` </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:142%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">math **import** add, subtract, multiply, divide</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(add(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => 3</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(subtract(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => 1</span>*

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895708160;margin-left:0px;margin-top:34px;width:967px;height:84px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image019.jpg" width="967" height="84" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">  </span></span>*<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This imports \`add\` and renames it to \`addSomeNumbers\` </span>***<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">from </span>**<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">math **import** add **as** addSomeNumbers</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(addSomeNumbers(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)) </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># => 3</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:14.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Python Learning Objectives (Day 3)</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895707136;margin-left:0px;margin-top:9px;width:967px;height:1px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image001.jpg" width="967" height="1" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Classes, methods, and properties</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895706112;margin-left:0px;margin-top:20px;width:967px;height:578px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image071.jpg" width="967" height="578" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">class </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#445588">AngryBird</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Slots optimize property access and memory usage</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">  </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">and prevent you from arbitrarily assigning new properties to the instance </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\_\_slots\_\_ = \[</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#DD1144">'\_x'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'\_y'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:134%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">constructor</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">\_\_init\_\_</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(self, x=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">0</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">, y=</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">0</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Doc string</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"""</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">Construct a new AngryBird by setting its position to (0, 0).</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">"""</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:128%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">## Instance variables </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:128%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">self.\_x = x self.\_y = y</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Instance method</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">move\_up\_by</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(self, delta):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">self.\_y += delta</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Getter</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

**<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@property </span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:132%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">x</span>**<span style="font-size:
6.5pt;line-height:132%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(self):</span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">self.\_x</span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Setter</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@x.setter</span>**

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">x</span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(self, value): **if** value &lt; </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">0</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:152%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">value = </span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:152%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">0</span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;
line-height:152%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> self.\_x = value</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@property</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">y</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(self):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">self.\_y</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999999">@y.setter</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">y</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(self, new\_y):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">self.\_y = new\_y</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">  </span></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Dunder Repr... called by \`print\` </span>***<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">def </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#990000">\_\_repr\_\_</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">(self):</span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">return </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">f"&lt;AngryBird (</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{self.\_x}</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">,</span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> </span>**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">{self.\_y}</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">)>"</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:10.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">JavaScript to Python Classes cheat table</span>**

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895705088;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:510px;height:241px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image072.jpg" width="510" height="241" /></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">

color:#333333">def \_\_init\_\_(self):</span>

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;

</span>

</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#333333">@someProperty.setter</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:12.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">List comprehensions</span>**

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">List comprehensions are a way to transform a list from one format to another.</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">They are a Pythonic alternative to using </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">map</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> or </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">filter</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> .</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895704064"><span style="position:absolute;left:196px;top:-13px;
width:82px;height:15px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image073.jpg" width="82" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Syntax of a list comprehension:</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895703040;margin-left:0px;margin-top:21px;width:187px;height:15px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image074.jpg" width="187" height="15" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">newList = \[value loop condition\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">Using a for loop</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895702016;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image032.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">squares = \[\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

**<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">for </span>**<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">i **in** range(</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">10</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">):</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">squares.append(i\*\*</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(squares)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Prints \[0, 1, 4, 9, 16, 25, 36, 49, 64, 81\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You can change it to a list comprehension</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif">  
</span>

<span id="page11"></span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;
color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span><span style="position:absolute;z-index:-1895700992;left:0px;margin-left:45px;
margin-top:37px;width:967px;height:110px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image032.jpg" width="967" height="110" /></span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">value = i \*\* 2</span>*

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"> </span>*

<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">  </span></span>*<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">loop = for i in range(10) </span>*<span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">squares = \[i\*\*</span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">2</span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333"> **for** i **in** range(</span><span style="font-size:6.5pt;line-height:
160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">10</span><span style="font-size:
6.5pt;line-height:160%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">)\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(list(squares))</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Prints \[0, 1, 4, 9, 16, 25, 36, 49, 64, 81\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">They can be used with a condition to do what </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">filter</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> does</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895699968;margin-left:0px;margin-top:18px;width:967px;height:97px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image010.jpg" width="967" height="97" /></span><span style="position:relative;z-index:-1895698944"><span style="position:absolute;
left:223px;top:-13px;width:41px;height:15px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image075.jpg" width="41" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">sentence = </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'the rocket came back from mars'</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">vowels = \[character **for** character **in** sentence **if** character **in** </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'aeiou'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">\]</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">print(vowels)</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988"># Prints \['e', 'o', 'e', 'a', 'e', 'a', 'o', 'a'\]</span>*

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">You can also use them on dictionaries. We can use the </span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">items()</span><span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;color:#333333"> method</span>

<span style="position:relative;
z-index:-1895697920"><span style="position:absolute;left:270px;top:-13px;
width:47px;height:15px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image076.jpg" width="47" height="15" /></span></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:8.5pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,sans-serif;
color:#333333">for the dictionary to loop through it getting the keys and values out at once.</span>

<span style="position:absolute;
z-index:-1895696896;margin-left:0px;margin-top:19px;width:967px;height:149px"><img src="w17-study-guide_files/image077.jpg" width="967" height="149" /></span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">person = {</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'name'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> 'Corina'</span><span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'age'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">32</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">,</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144">'height'</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">:</span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#DD1144"> </span><span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:teal">1.4</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;
font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">}</span>

<span style="font-size:10.0pt"> </span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">This loops through and capitalizes the first letter of all the keys </span>*<span style="font-size:7.0pt;line-height:122%;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#333333">newPerson = { key.title(): value **for** key, value **in** person.items() }</span>

<span style="font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">#<span style="font:7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;"> </span></span>*<span style="font-size:
7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Courier New&quot;;color:#999988">Prints {'Name': 'Corina', 'Age': 32, 'Height': 1.4}</span>*
